 After the constitution came into force in 1950, the first general elections were held in the country in 1951, which lasted till 1952
 oktober 1951 main aam chunaav kii prakriya shuru hui jo paanch maheene tak chali or farvari 1952 main khatm hui
 For the first time when elections were held, votes were cast for a total of 4500 seats, out of which 489 were for Lok Sabha and the rest were Assembly seats
 1951 ke aam chunaav main 14 rashtriya party, 39 rajya str kii party or nirdaleey ummidavaaron ne kismat aajamaai
 a total of 1874 candidates of all these parties were trying their luck
 rashtriya partiyon main mukhya taur par congress, sipiai, bhartiya jansangh or baba sahib ambedkar kii party shaamil thi
 Apart from this, parties like Akali Dal and Forward Bloc had joined the election
 loksabhaa kii 489 siton main se 364 congress ke khate main gai thim, yani jawahar laal nehru kii aguwai main congress ko sampurna bahumat mila tha
 After the Congress, the CPI became the second largest party with 16 seats, with the Socialist Party winning 12 and 37 seats won by independents
 bhartiya jansangh ne 94 siton par chunaav ladaa or teen hi siten jeetin
 There were a total of 17 crore voters during the first election, but the turnout was only 44 per cent
 chune gaye 489 saansadon main se 391 saamaanya, 72 essi or 26 asti jati se the
 At that time the voting age was not even 18 years, only people above 21 years were allowed to vote
 pehle chunaav ke samay sukumaar sen desh ke pehle chunaav ayukta the, chunaav karwaane ke liye chunaav ayog ko bhi kaaphi mashkkat kerani padi thi
 Then there was no fight over evms, as there was no other option to impose stamps and vote with ballot paper
 pehle chunaav main dhai lakh matdaan centre bane, saadhe saat lakh ballat box banaae gaye, teen lakh se zyada syaahi ke pakaton kaa istemaal hua
 Not only this, the Election Commission had to employ about 16000 people under contract for 6 months
 tab desh kii sakshartaa kaaphi kam thi, isliye ayog kii taraf se gaanv-gaanv main nukkad naatak karvaa kar logon ko vot daalane ke liye kaha gaya

 piie ke pravaktaa danial gilaani ne kaha ki vimaan main 42 yatri, chaalak dal ke paanch sadsy or ek ground ejeeniyar savaar the
 According to the list of people aboard the plane, it had 31 men, nine women and two infants
 inamen se teen videshi naagarik hai
 The official said, "the wreckage of the aircraft has been found
 abhi tak kisi ke jivit bache hone kaa sanket nahin he'
 a senior aviation official said that the engine of the aircraft had malfunctioned
 islamabad hawaondde par samvaadadaataaon se baatcheet main vimaanan sachiv irfan ilaahi ne pushti kii he ki atiar-42 vimaan main ingine sambandhi dikkat aayi thi
 He said, "it is too early to say anything, but we know that there was a problem in the engine of the aircraft"
 nagar vimaanan kshetra main hone vaale haadason or apaat sthiti par rojaanaa suchanaaen dene vaale akhbaar 'aviation herald' ne bhi kaha tha ki vimaan ke 'ingine main dikkat' thi
 The newspaper quoted local government sources as saying that the chances of anyone surviving the accident are 'very weak'
 piie ke ek pravaktaa ne 'express news' se kaha ki kareeb '10 saal purana yah vimaan acchhee haalat main tha'
 Junaid Jamshed's brother told the media that his brother and sister-in-law and other members of the tabligi (religious group) were aboard the plane
 sabhi chitral kii dharmik yatra se laut rahe the
 inter-services Public Relations says that the Army contingent and the helicopter have been dispatched to the spot
 rashtriya aapadaa prabandhan prakoshth ke ek varisht adhikari aabid ali kaa kahana he ki bachaav kaary jari he or chah helicopteron ko madad ke liye lagaaya gaya he
 Since the accident has happened in the mountainous region, it will take some time to remove debris and remove dead bodies
 vimaan shuru main peshawar se chitral gaya tha or vahaan se islamabad vaapasi ke dauraan radar se gaayab ho gaya
 According to media reports, eyewitnesses say that they have seen a plane crash in the hill near Havelian
 vahaan se dhuen kaa gubbaar uth rahaa tha
 The comments bayaan ke anusaar, pradhanmantri navaj sharif ne abhi adhikariyon ko nirdesh diya he ki ve turant maukey par pahunchen or raahat evam bachaav kaary shuru karen
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) vimaan buudhvaar shaam pakistan ke chhavnee shahar abtabad ke najadik ek pahari ilaake main durghatnagrast hua
 On the way to Chitral from Islamabad to Khabar Pakhtunkhwa province, a PIA plane PK-661 crashed in Patola village near Pakistan Ordnance Factory in Havelian
 vimaan main junayd jamshed, unki patni or chitral ke upayukta osama varich sahit kul 48 log savaar the
 The Civil Aviation Authority has confirmed that there are no survivors
 abhi tak malbe se 36 shav nikaale gaye hai
 Pakistan's National Aviation Service took off from Chitral at 3:30 pm and was to land at Benazir Bhutto International Airport in Islamabad at around 4:40 pm
 sena ke anusaar, durghatanasthal se abhi tak 21 shav nikaale gaye hai
 a PIA spokesperson confirmed that the pilot of the aircraft had given 'emergency information' to the traffic controller before the aircraft was taken off the radar
 piie ke pravaktaa danial gilaani ne kaha ki vimaan main 42 yatri, chaalak dal ke paanch sadsy or ek ground ejeeniyar savaar the
 According to the list of people aboard the plane, it had 31 men, nine women and two infants
 inamen se teen videshi naagarik hai
 The official said, "the wreckage of the aircraft has been found
 abhi tak kisi ke jivit bache hone kaa sanket nahin he'
 a senior aviation official said that the engine of the aircraft had malfunctioned
 islamabad hawaondde par samvaadadaataaon se baatcheet main vimaanan sachiv irfan ilaahi ne pushti kii he ki atiar-42 vimaan main ingine sambandhi dikkat aayi thi
 He said, "it is too early to say anything, but we know that there was a problem in the engine of the aircraft"
 nagar vimaanan kshetra main hone vaale haadason or apaat sthiti par rojaanaa suchanaaen dene vaale akhbaar 'aviation herald' ne bhi kaha tha ki vimaan ke 'ingine main dikkat' thi
 The newspaper quoted local government sources as saying that the chances of anyone surviving the accident are 'very weak'
 piie ke ek pravaktaa ne 'express news' se kaha ki kareeb '10 saal purana yah vimaan acchhee haalat main tha'
 Junaid Jamshed's brother told the media that his brother and sister-in-law and other members of the tabligi (religious group) were aboard the plane
 sabhi chitral kii dharmik yatra se laut rahe the
 inter-services Public Relations says that the Army contingent and the helicopter have been dispatched to the spot
 rashtriya aapadaa prabandhan prakoshth ke ek varisht adhikari aabid ali kaa kahana he ki bachaav kaary jari he or chah helicopteron ko madad ke liye lagaaya gaya he
 Since the accident has happened in the mountainous region, it will take some time to remove debris and remove dead bodies
 vimaan shuru main peshawar se chitral gaya tha or vahaan se islamabad vaapasi ke dauraan radar se gaayab ho gaya
 According to media reports, eyewitnesses say that they have seen a plane crash in the hill near Havelian
 vahaan se dhuen kaa gubbaar uth rahaa tha
 The comments bayaan ke anusaar, pradhanmantri navaj sharif ne abhi adhikariyon ko nirdesh diya he ki ve turant maukey par pahunchen or raahat evam bachaav kaary shuru karen
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) khabar pakhtoonkhwaa praant main chitral se islamabad jate samay piie kaa vimaan pike-661 haweliyaan sthit pakistan ayuddh factory ke paas patola gaanv main durghatnagrast ho gaya
 a total of 48 people were in the aircraft, including Junaid Jamshed, his wife and Chitral Deputy Commissioner Osama Varaich
 nagar vimaanan praadhikaran ne pushti kii he ki koi jivit nahin bachaa he
 So far, 36 bodies have been recovered from the debris
 pakistan kii rashtriya vimaanan seva ne is vimaan ne dopaher 3:30 baje chitral se udaan bhari thi or shaam kareeb 4:40 baje ise islamabad ke benazir bhutto antarrashtriya hawaondde par utarana tha
 According to the army, 21 bodies have so far been recovered from the accident site
 piie ke ek pravaktaa ne pushti kii he ki is vimaan ke radar se hatane se pehle vimaan ke payalat ne yatayaat niyantrak ko 'apaat sthiti sambandhi soochna' di thi
 PIA spokesman Daniel Gilani said the aircraft carried 42 passengers, five crew members and a ground engineer
 vimaan main savaar logon kii suchi ke anusaar, usamen 31 purush, nau mahilaayein or do shishu the
 Three of them are foreign nationals
 adhikari ne kaha, 'vimaan kaa malba mil gaya he
 There is no sign of any survivor yet '
 vimaanan kshetra ke ek varisht adhikari ne kaha ki vimaan ke ingine main kharabi aa gai thi
 Speaking to reporters at the Islamabad airport, Aviation Secretary Irfan Elahi confirmed that the ATR-42 aircraft had engine problems
 unhone kaha, 'abhi kuch bhi kahana jaldibaji hogi, lekin ham jaanate hai ki vimaan ke ingine main dikkat ai thi'
 The newspaper 'aviation Herald', which provided daily information on accidents and emergencies in the civil aviation sector, also said that the aircraft had 'engine problems'
 akhbaar ne sthaneey sarkari sutron ke hawaale se kaha ki haadase main kisi ke jivit bache hone kii sambhaavna 'bahut ksheen' he
 a PIA spokesperson told 'express News' that the '10-year-old aircraft was in good condition'
 junayd jamshed ke bhai ne media se kaha ki vimaan main unke bhai or bhabhi tathaa tabaligi (dharmik samooh) ke anya sadsy savaar the
 All were returning from a religious visit to Chitral
 inter-services public relations kaa kahana he ki sena kii tukdi or helicopter ko maukey par ravaanaa kar diya gaya he
 Abid Ali, a senior official of the National Disaster Management Cell, says rescue operations are on and six helicopters have been pressed into service
 chunki haadasa parvatiy kshetra main hua he, aise main malbe ko hataane tathaa shavon ko nikaalane main kuch vakt lagegaa
 The aircraft initially flew from Peshawar to Chitral and disappeared from the radar while returning to Islamabad
 media main aayi khabaron ke anusaar, pratyakshdarshiyon kaa kahana he ki unhone haweliyaan ke nikat pahari main ek vimaan ko durghatnagrast hote hue dekha he
 a balloon of smoke was rising from there
 tippaniyan According to the statement, Prime Minister Nawaz Sharif has now directed officials to immediately reach the spot and start rescue and relief operations
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he

 What Mohan Bhagwat has said is not new
 pehali baar nahin kaha he

 mohan bhagwat ne kaha he ki puri duniya bharatiyon ko hindu maanati he, isliye bharat ek hindu raashtra he
 If there is English living in England, German living in Germany, American living in America, then those who live in Hindustan are Hindus
 amareeki, english kii tarah ham bhartiya kyon nahin hai? ham indian kyon nahin hai? ham hindu hi kyon hai? kya sikh, musmalaan, isai, parsi bhi hindu hai? phir ve sikh kyon hai, musalmaan kyon hai, parsi kyon hai? kya bhagwat ke sabhi hindustaniyon ko hindu kehane se baaki mazahabon main apni pahchaan ko lekar koi bhram kii sthiti paidaa hoti he yaa vah kuch or kah rahe hai

 In this new system, an encrypted ballot with unique code will be used instead of ballot paper
 iske jariye voter ko yah jaankaree ho sakegi ki unhone kise vot daalaa or unka vot kise gaya he

 Sharing of photos on Facebook has become a trade and now in the era of selfie, photo is not clicked here that the next moment it gets uploaded on Facebook
 ye baat kisi se chhipi nahin he ki fasebuk par photo aplod karnaa khatarnaak ho saktaa he baavjood iske ham fasebuk par photose aplod karne kaa ek bhi mauka nahin chhodte
 We not only upload pictures of ourselves, we also upload photos of our children
 lekin kya aap jaanate hai fasebuk par bacchon kii photose aplod karnaa kitna khatarnaak ho saktaa he
 
 
 Don't forget to upload these seven pictures of children to Facebook
 
 
 1
 Such a picture in which the child is bathing, there are many parents who share the picture of the bath time of the child on Facebook
 mana ki nahaate vakt aapkaa baccha bahut kute lag rahaa hoga or aap is pal ko hameshaa ke liye kaid kar lenaa chaahate honge lekin use fasebuk par share karnaa bilkul galat idia he
 It is not right to put a naked picture of the child on social media
 ho saktaa he ye mument aapke liye bahut yaadgaar ho lekin fasebuk par peadophiles bhi hote hai
 This picture of your child can serve to give them a chance
 2
 It is also not right to share personal details, it can be dangerous to share your home number, your society name, your child's school name, his age and details related to his nanny on Facebook
 ye personal ditels aapke bachche ke liye khatra sabit ho sakati hai
 3
 bachche ke poti training ke dauraan lee gai tasveerenbhache kii aisi tasviren galati se bhi share na karen
 Right now he may be small but when he grows up, these pictures can embarrass him
 ye behad nijee tasviren hai
 It is not right to share them on Facebook
 4
 Such a picture of a child in which he is seen as embarrassed, sharing such pictures is not yet but it can be harmful for you in future
 ho saktaa he ki future main in tasveeron ko fasebuk par dekhakar aapke bachche kaa bharosa tut jaae or wo aapse nafrat karne lage
 It may also happen that he goes into depression
 5
 Group Photos: If you also put the pictures of the birthday party on Facebook, then stop doing so now
 ho saktaa he ki aapako isamen koi buraai najar nahin aati ho lekindusre bacchon ke parents ko isse problem ho sakati he
 In such a situation, be careful while sharing pictures of the birthday party of the child
 6
 Picture of the injury or illness of the child
 Imagine yourself lying in bed and someone insists on taking a selfie with you and taking a photo and posting it, how would you feel? Children are small but they also have feelings and they may feel bad
 7
 Photos of Unsafe Activities If you take a photo in a moving car or take a selfie with your child while posing on the banks of a river, first stop doing so
 aisa karnaa khatarnaak ho saktaa he
 Also, do not share these pictures on Facebook at all
 aisi tasviren baikaphire kar sakati hai
